To which he replied "The pulled pork KC style BBQ" sandwich with potato salad and a bag of chips.  He was not wrong.  The meat and BBQ sauce were D-E-licious! The buns were soft and absorbed some of the juice from the meat and sauce.  But one of my favorite things about my visit was the decor.  Awards hang on the wall from the many BBQ contests that they have won and Fred himself is quiet, humble and almost stand off-ish, but not in a bad way.  I felt as if his personality made the atmosphere with that crooked smile. Like a cowboy.
Some may take him as a difficult person to know- Hey you're there to eat the food not the owner.  I see him as a BBQ mastermind and they even serve Cactus Coolers.  My all-time fav soda!!!  They do boxed lunches for kid's sports and executive board meetings or a nice picnic.
My thing is to order 2 sandwiches.... One for me and one for.... Well, a midnight snack for ME!
5 STARS - ALL DAY - EVERY DAY!<//text>< gmapID>

0x808e34fd99f4dfdd:0x2999ed181dcf9add</Gmap_id>
< review>
Clean, dry, well-run location with units on three levels, some climate-controlled.  Friendly, competent folks in the office.  Always helpful.
The units are used by businesses and individuals, including of course a few homeless folks -- I've never felt unsafe, even with my NYC-trained spidey-senses. You need your code to both get in and to get out, and the elevator areas have video cameras at each level.  I wish the gates were open past 9:30 or 10 pm,, but that seems pretty standard..

There are three sets of exterior doors and elevators,, two of of which have covered loading docks (including a recessed dock which seems built for U-hauls; not high enough for a full-size moving van).  When moving in/out you can reserve a spot to simplify logistics.. Plenty of dollies stored inside -- you just use and return, no need to waste time checking out a dolly by handing over a drivers license.  Occasionally one of the elevators doesn't work, but it turns out the building is interconnected well so that's actually not a problem.

The only reason for four stars is the prices.  At least you're charged from the day you rent, not from the first of the month like in some other places. All levels have clean air, no musty smells. Overall, a very well-run place.<//review>

We Have been looking for a new shop since our old one closed. stopped at Cannavine up the road first And was horribly disappointed so we decided to drive up the road to Revolution. Immediately I could tell this was a good place. It‚Äôs small and surrounded by plants which had been labeled with different terpene names. Obviously knowledgeable üëç Couldn‚Äôt go inside because of covid but was greeted warmly by the male bud tender at a small window. He showed us the sign of what was available and the ounce and half ounce deals. We asked if we could see the actual weed and he said some of it was in solid containers so you can‚Äôt see through them. He then told us about the cannabis inside, letting us know the look, smell and sharing he had tried it and it was really good. He obviously was very knowledgeable about the dispensaries  products and was a great help. This is a cash only shop but they do have an atm in the back you can use, one person at a time. This shop has a nice welcoming vibe and good prices for chronic weed. Sales tax is about 7 and a half % which is great seeing as Mendocann in hopland is 30%. Definitely making this our go to shop and I highly recommended it to anyone looking for good cannabis and good customer service.</review>

The room itself was clean. However the guest service is motel6 style service. 4 of 5 times I have tried to reach the front desk there is no answer. When I checked in I had to call the attendant's personal cell phone. she came rushing out of a guests room. Is she providing "additional services"? That is what the perception is. They charge an extra $50 in case you decide you like the towels and sheets more than your own at home. I was told this would be refunded when I checked out. Almost a week later it has not been refunded. With my rewards level I am able to have a late check out. When I asked how this worked the attendant responded in such a way that I felt like I was asking her to provide the same "additional services" the check in attendant was providing! <Review>Sundowner Inn or as it is now called, Days Inn by Wyndham, is a centrally located Inn right off Hwy 237 in Sunnyvale. Due to it's prime lication, commuters have quick access (by car) to all of Silicon Valley. The rooms are spacious and spotless, and have been recently renovated. I found my stay very comfortable. There are also wheelchair accessible rooms with great care taken to ensure full amenities and easy accessibility features (room 107 is a great example). Mr. Shah, the owner, continues to help his staff regularly, with the vigor and vim of a person a quarter of his age , even sometimes working the front desk on weekends, where he loves to meet his guests and give them an overview of the grounds, of which he takes great pride. There is a lovely pool on-site and breakfast is served daily at the pool cabana. There is also a Greek restaurant with tasty choices for everyone. <UserId.>115588798835511682572</UserId.><rating>1<//rating>< review>
I ended up spending the nights of Monday - Thursday at the Days Inn in Sunnyvale.  It was the only thing that was close, still available, and under the hotel cap for my company, so I went for it.  I didn't realize it was a motel (strike 1), I didn't realize it was itty-bitty (strike 2), or that it didn't have wifi (strike 3), so I wasn't terribly happy on first arrival.  That night, I was made less happy by being woken up twice by loud rodent sounds coming from roughly under my bed.  Gross, but fine, I thought, I'll just make sure I eat all my meals out, not leave food anywhere, and not spend much time here until tomorrow night, when I can get my money back.

Except they wouldn't let me leave.  They told me first that I couldn't get a refund for the first night, which I thought was lousy but reasonable.  I had paid them for a night in a room, I guess I didn't specify it needed to be rat-free.  Then they told me that I couldn't get my money back for that night, or any of the other nights I was staying there.  "You can leave any time you like, but you can never check out," I guess.  I was pretty resigned at this point, so I asked if they could at least get me some traps I can set so I can sleep.  They said, and I quote this because it is so memorable, "We had the guy buy extra traps this week, but it looks like we're out."  Every part of that sentence is just wrong.  You cannot run a motel under these circumstances.  But no, resigned Nathan just asks if they can direct me to a hardware store so I can buy my own traps.  I figure I'll expense them!  I get the name of one down the street and she prints out Google Maps directions for me.  I follow the Google Maps directions, arrive at the hardware store: it's closed.

So I gave up and coped with it.  The second night I was there I finally got a glimpse of one of these. It was about the size of a soda can and was running from behind my nightstand to behind my bed.  Ugh.<//review>

< Review>
This seems like a good deal for the price compared to other Santa Clara hotels and motels. The check-in experience could have been better, I think the 'new guy' checked me in. <time>1398237352307</time><Rate>1<//Rate>< Text>
I'm sitting in the room right now, debating if I can make it through the night hiding on top of this bed or if I need to go find another room or even sleep in the car. This is by far the worst hotel I've ever been in.
The front desk lady must have been depressed. Checked my friend into my room and me into his and told us to just not cause any issues in the rooms.
In the room, the lights all have sensors on the switches so the lights keep randomly turning on and off. There are cobwebs in the corners, black stains on the walls and the floor boards in the bathroom have all been torn out (probably due to the water damage under the sink).
The sheets and blankets look clean, but of course I'm too freaked out to look at the mattress under them. So I'm going to sleep on top of the blanket and use the blanket from the other bed next to me to keep me warm (this is again assuming I don't hear bugs crawling and abandon everything and sleep in the car).
So much for Days Inn having any semblance of a reliable brand. Avoid this place like it's the plague.</Text>

< review>
EDIT 1/31/2018: I have to say I am super happy with Target for listening to their customers! Ever since my review 8 months ago the shelves are stocked and cleaned regularly, in fact there were plenty of boxes of Pokemon TCG that were quite a few generations back so we were able to finish our collections without paying surcharged prices due to the age of generation. The boxes of stock have been moved out of the front checkout area of the collectibles aisle. The bathrooms have been cleaned up as well which is a major plus for me. Customer service is still great. And the helpfullness and stock is always above and beyond. Thanks Target!

Target is a convenient place for me to shop when I need to grab baby items, groceries, and a few other miscellaneous items. This Target in particular is easy to navigate and generally well stocked with the items I need. However, there are a couple area's that could use some improvement. For instance, you can tell when an area has been given a blind eye due to it's location, my husband collects Pokemon cards and it seems that the two areas that carry these cards are hardly stocked, usually disheveled with card packs not being in the right place, and cramped with empty boxes or carts strewn about the aisles and shelves. I could understand packs not being on the right hooks because there are usually children who look through these, however when your shopping experience is hindered because you have to sift through empty boxes, or push multiple carts out of an already cramped space it makes it feel like you went into the backroom where the stock is kept, and to see the same mess on different days, it makes you wonder if they give any attention to these two locations. Secondly, the bathrooms are always a wreck. I have never seen restrooms so messed up. Again, I can understand after a rush, or maybe because of the holidays, but again when you come to your local Target and see the same mess over several days it makes you wonder how much time they devote to such a private and public place. Overall customer service is good, you can get fast assistance when you need it, and the clerks are always attentive.</review>
